  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_279cd43c-e5ba-4b3e-b459-c6cb7c469063'

<span id="freeTextContainer15610338745607683801">Tutup mata kita. Tutup pikiran kita dari carut- marut kehidupan. Mari berpikir takjim sejenak.   <span id="freeText15610338745607683801" style="display:none">Tutup mata kita. Tutup pikiran kita dari carut- marut kehidupan. Mari berpikir takjim sejenak. Bayangkan saat ini ada satu malaikat bersayap indah datang kepada kita, lantas lembut berkata: Aku memberikan kau kesempatan hebat. Lima kesempatan untuk bertanya tentang rahasia kehidupan, dan aku akan menjawabnya langsung sekarang. Lima Pertanyaan. Lima jawaban. Apakah pertanyaan pertamamu? <br />Maka apakah kita akan bertanya: Apakah cinta itu? Apakah hidup ini adil? Apakah kaya adalah segalanya? Apakah kita memilki pilihan dalam hidup? Apakah makna kehilangan?<br />Ray (tokoh utama dalam kisah ini), ternyata memiliki kecamuk pertanyaan sendiri. Lima pertanyaan sebelum akhirnya dia mengerti makna hidup dan kehidupannya.<br />Siapkan energi Anda untuk memasuki dunia Fantasi Tere-Liye tentang perjalanan hidup. Di sini hanya ada satu rumus: semua urusan adalah sederhana. Maka mulailah membaca dengan menghela nafas lega</span>
  <a data-text-id="15610338745607683801" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4602279437307583099">"an awesome book for an awesome person" <br/>written by a friend in the first page of the book<br/>"u must read it...." she said.<br/><br/>well,<br/>i do under estimate the book at first. The title, the cover design....really not my type<br/>its only because i already gave my promised to read it.<br/><br/>but what i found behind all that i categorize as "not my type", is something different.<br/><br/>if u ever watch WANTED, then i hope you will agree with me if i said that the moral message in this book is almost <br/>similar with what the movie sai</span>
  <span id="freeText4602279437307583099" style="display:none">"an awesome book for an awesome person" <br />written by a friend in the first page of the book<br />"u must read it...." she said.<br /><br />well,<br />i do under estimate the book at first. The title, the cover design....really not my type<br />its only because i already gave my promised to read it.<br /><br />but what i found behind all that i categorize as "not my type", is something different.<br /><br />if u ever watch WANTED, then i hope you will agree with me if i said that the moral message in this book is almost <br />similar with what the movie said. <br /><br />the idea is about how we,connected each others...<br />about how what we do, connect and influenced others...weaved each other in a complex relations.<br /><br />almost, i said.<br />because The Fraternity in WANTED interpretate those connection with arrogance.<br />sounds silly if they thought they had a right to kill others, only based on weaving errors of the fabric.<br /><br />while the book, interpretate in a humble.<br />and said that those connectivity is always meaningfull<br />that no matter how small it is, what we do is affect others. <br />that every question has an answer.<br />only if you could just open your heart.<br />Because live is fair. Always fair.<br />Because HE is there. Always there.<br /><br />read it, <br />open your heart.<br />and you will know what i mean.<br /><br />best part :<br />"kalau Tuhan menginginkannnya terjadi, maka sebuah kejadian pasti terjadi, tidak peduli seluruh isi langit-bumi bersekutu menggagalkannya....Sebeliknya, kalau Tuhan tidak menginginkannya,maka sebuah kejadian niscaya tidak akan terjadi, tak peduli seluruh isi langit-bumi bersekutu melaksanakannya...<br />Kejadian buruk itu datang sesuai takdir langit...hanya ada satu hal yang bisa mencegahnya...satu hal!sama seperti siklus sebab-akibat sebelumnya, yaitu berbagi!. Ya, berbagi apa saja dengan orang lain. Tidak, sebenarnya berbagi tidak bisa mencegahnya secara langsung, tetapi dengan berbagi, kau akan membuat hatimu damai...hanya orang - orang dengan hati damailah yang bisa menerima kejadian buruk dengan lega. <br />hanya orang - orang berhati damailah."<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_746548848" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/746548848" />
    <a title="Boy Al Idrus" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10349383-boy-al-idrus"><img alt="Boy Al Idrus" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1340180487p2/10349383.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/746548848?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Boy Al Idrus" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Boy Al Idrus" href="/user/show/10349383-boy-al-idrus">Boy Al Idrus</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer746548848" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14079876117896689607">If i need to explain you the reasons why i gave five stars for this book, indeed there will be so much of them to be elaborated. I like this book, i really do. <br/><br/>When we talk about books, it's going to get back to us, everyone has their different intention of reading books, maybe reading books kills your time or, reading books saves you from your annoying fellows, the point is, my interpretation of this book is going to be so personal since it's very clear, we all have of our different perspective</span>
  <span id="freeText14079876117896689607" style="display:none">If i need to explain you the reasons why i gave five stars for this book, indeed there will be so much of them to be elaborated. I like this book, i really do. <br /><br />When we talk about books, it's going to get back to us, everyone has their different intention of reading books, maybe reading books kills your time or, reading books saves you from your annoying fellows, the point is, my interpretation of this book is going to be so personal since it's very clear, we all have of our different perspectives at the end. <br /><br />When i got this book on my hand for the first time, I was awkward by the title, it's a romantic-like story or what? to be honest, the title is not that actually representing the story, it's more than that, and i am sure i could find more better title. okay, forget it. lol.<br /><br />the story is actually simple, of one man that struggles his life within the very-circular-life-dynamics. what makes it different from other novel is how close the story can get into you. the details (i would say that) are very precise, and tere liye can make you feel your self like was in the story. <br /><br />The characters, no doubt are strongly-written. after all, yes it is a fiction, but it's not going to be hard to imagine you find someone like in the novel in your usual life, i can say the characters are engaging yet understandable. <br /><br />The message of the story, well... is the power of this novel. I refresh my self a lot after reading this book, (thou I think i am still the same person yet, :P) but the message will clearly crash your mind, i am sure. I like all the answers for all the heavy questions of this novel, such as is this life a fair one? and others. <br /><br />I recommend this book. definitely. <br /><br /><br /></span>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer5092419140814326272">bismillah.<br/><br/>rembulan tenggelam di wajahmu. at first I thought it was just another typical love story (without reading the synopsis), but reading through it and falling in love with its character, i realized that it was not a love story. nope. probably the only love story you could find was the relationship between ray and fitri (and i assure you their story was much better than romeo and juliet).<br/><br/>the whole novel revolved around the life of ray or rehan. in summary, ray, being a human being, while f</span>
  <span id="freeText5092419140814326272" style="display:none">bismillah.<br /><br />rembulan tenggelam di wajahmu. at first I thought it was just another typical love story (without reading the synopsis), but reading through it and falling in love with its character, i realized that it was not a love story. nope. probably the only love story you could find was the relationship between ray and fitri (and i assure you their story was much better than romeo and juliet).<br /><br />the whole novel revolved around the life of ray or rehan. in summary, ray, being a human being, while facing ups and downs in life, realized that maybe the sky (it's a metaphor) was just too cruel to him. despite his extreme hostility towards the sky, he has this one affection and attachment towards rembulan. he adores it very much and find solace in staring to it every single night.<br /><br />it is a very good novel, a great masterpiece. you will fall in love with ray and at the same time symphatise with him. in the middle of the novel, when all misfortunes seemed to befall him, even you yourself would start questioning the sky.<br /><br />the novel gives me a lot of insights in life. one is to believe in Allah's decree, because no matter how hard it seems to be in our eyes, know that what Allah had decide for us is the best for us in both worlds. <br /><br />some of my favourite excerpts from the book:<br /><br />"Orang-orang yang memiliki tujuan hidup, tahu persis apa yg hendak dicapainya, maka baginya semua kesedihan yang dialaminya adalah tempaan, harga tujuan tersebut. Dan sebaliknya."<br /><br />"Begitulah kehidupan, Ada yang kita tahu, ada pula yang tidak kita tahu. Yakinlah, dengan ketidak-tahuan itu bukan berarti Tuhan berbuat jahat kepada kita. Mungkin saja Tuhan sengaja melindungi kita dari tahu itu sendiri."<br /><br />highly recommended! :)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4296592121605378882">Rembulan Tenggelam di Wajah Mu is a novel written by tere liye. This novel is very popular among teenagers.<br/> The novel Rembulan tenggelam di wajah mu is very interesting, although at first it was a bit confusing because it uses a third-person perspective, where the narrator knows everything with all the roles that appear suddenly in each chapter, and who is then able to answer 5 questions with 5 answers , through past travel opportunities. This novel initially also tells a few characters, but onl</span>
  <span id="freeText4296592121605378882" style="display:none">Rembulan Tenggelam di Wajah Mu is a novel written by tere liye. This novel is very popular among teenagers.<br /> The novel Rembulan tenggelam di wajah mu is very interesting, although at first it was a bit confusing because it uses a third-person perspective, where the narrator knows everything with all the roles that appear suddenly in each chapter, and who is then able to answer 5 questions with 5 answers , through past travel opportunities. This novel initially also tells a few characters, but only appears at the beginning and then disappears, and appears again in the last chapter. Remarkably, the character is related to the main character "Ray".<br /> This novel tells about the life journey of a young child, who is very winding. The journey of life that always raises questions about life. Although at the beginning of the story the plot seems boring, and confused because of the jump plot but<br /> This novel is somewhat unique, because this novel uses the perspective of an all-knowing third person. Quite confusing, but it makes the reader curious about all kinds of grooves conveyed. This novel teaches what is meant by gratitude, simplicity, sincerity, and respect for what we already have. This novel also really invites us to go into the world of fantasy, fantasizing about following the storyline.<br /> This causes the reader to always wait for what will happen next.<br /> The author uses a very good diction selection, so we are taken as if he is feeling what the character feels. The depiction of the atmosphere feels very perfect and real. I strongly encourage you to read this book and feel the sensations and atmosphere felt after reading it.</span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mFc6T0J0kl06Tg3VL60F7T7jS/zQQ4A9GiLm+7HkEeAJxVP1EiyV+Cyh2B+RjEX50sIlIyBB2DbVoQREqn27zA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+aZhvv3wF48TSvW8aAI65jbdYywm1pFkiP8Weg8WtO1oNAgEragQKgWlIHbWI3ry2vwN89bUyW9HfPTFFI8ewQ==')})
  }

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_6688121'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6688121-negeri-5-menara?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Negeri 5 Menara<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/3012699.Ahmad_Fuadi?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Ahmad Fuadi<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.10 avg rating &mdash; 12,010 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2009\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer6320098610342054771\">Alif lahir di pinggir Danau Maninjau dan tidak pernah menginjak tanah di luar ranah Minangkabau. Masa kecilnya adalah berburu durian runtuh di rimba Bukit Barisan, bermain bola di sawah berlumpur dan tentu mandi berkecipak di air biru Danau Maninjau.<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText6320098610342054771\" style=\"display:none\">Alif lahir di pinggir Danau Maninjau dan tidak pernah menginjak tanah di luar ranah Minangkabau. Masa kecilnya adalah berburu durian runtuh di rimba Bukit Barisan, bermain bola di sawah berlumpur dan tentu mandi berkecipak di air biru Danau Maninjau.\n\nTiba-tiba saja dia harus naik bus tiga hari tiga malam melintasi punggung Sumatera dan Jawa menuju sebuah desa di pelosok Jawa Timur. Ibunya ingin dia menjadi Buya Hamka walau Alif ingin menjadi Habibie. Dengan setengah hati dia mengikuti perintah Ibunya: belajar di pondok.\n\nDi kelas hari pertamanya di Pondok Madani (PM), Alif terkesima dengan “mantera” sakti man jadda wajada. Siapa yang bersungguh-sungguh pasti sukses.\n\nDia terheran-heran mendengar komentator sepakbola berbahasa Arab, anak menggigau dalam bahasa Inggris, merinding mendengar ribuan orang melagukan Syair Abu Nawas dan terkesan melihat pondoknya setiap pagi seperti melayang di udara.\n\nDipersatukan oleh hukuman jewer berantai, Alif berteman dekat dengan Raja dari Medan, Said dari Surabaya, Dulmajid dari Sumenep, Atang dari Bandung dan Baso dari Gowa. Di bawah menara masjid yang menjulang, mereka berenam kerap menunggu maghrib sambil menatap awan lembayung yang berarak pulang ke ufuk. Di mata belia mereka, awan-awan itu menjelma menjadi negara dan benua impian masing-masing. Kemana impian jiwa muda ini membawa mereka? Mereka tidak tahu. Yang mereka tahu adalah: Jangan pernah remehkan impian, walau setinggi apa pun. Tuhan sungguh Maha Mendengar.\n\nBagaimana perjalanan mereka ke ujung dunia ini dimulai? Siapa horor nomor satu mereka? Apa pengalaman mendebarkan di tengah malam buta di sebelah sungai tempat jin buang anak? Bagaimana sampai ada yang kasak-kusuk menjadi mata-mata misterius? Siapa Princess of Madani yang mereka kejar-kejar? Kenapa mereka harus botak berkilat-kilat? Bagaimana sampai Icuk Sugiarto, Arnold Schwarzenegger, Ibnu Rusyd, bahkan Maradona sampai akhirnya ikut campur? Ikuti perjalanan hidup yang inspiratif ini langsung dari mata para pelakunya. Negeri Lima Menara adalah buku pertama dari sebuah trilogi.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"6320098610342054771\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n       <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/1366035-rembulan-tenggelam-di-wajahmu">Quotes from Rembulan Tenggela...</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Begitulah kehidupan, Ada yang kita tahu, ada pula yang tidak kita tahu. Yakinlah, dengan ketidak-tahuan itu bukan berarti Tuhan berbuat jahat kepada kita. Mungkin saja Tuhan sengaja melindungi kita dari tahu itu sendiri.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/485354-begitulah-kehidupan-ada-yang-kita-tahu-ada-pula-yang-tidak">391 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Bagi manusia, hidup itu juga sebab-akibat, Ray. Bedanya, bagi manusia sebab-akibat itu membentuk peta dengan ukuran raksasa. Kehidupanmu menyebabkan perubahan garis kehidupan orang lain, kehidupan orang lain mengakibatkan perubahan garis kehidupan orang lainnya lagi, kemudian entah pada siklus yang keberapa, kembali lagi ke garis kehidupanmu.... Saling mempengaruhi, saling berinteraksi.... Sungguh kalau kulukiskan peta itu maka ia bagai bola raksasa dengan benang jutaan warna yang saling melilit, saling menjalin, lingkar-melingkar. Indah. Sungguh indah. Sama sekali tidak rumit.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/358001-bagi-manusia-hidup-itu-juga-sebab-akibat-ray-bedanya-bagi-manusia">267 likes</a>
